<span data-ttu-id="b50a3-1032">Questa classe contiene gli attributi seguenti per Windows Server 2003 R2:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b50a3-1032">This class contains the following attributes for Windows Server 2003 R2:</span></span>



| <span data-ttu-id="b50a3-1033">Attributo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b50a3-1033">Attribute</span></span>                                                                    | <span data-ttu-id="b50a3-1034">Obbligatorio</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b50a3-1034">Mandatory</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="b50a3-1035">Derivato da</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b50a3-1035">Derived from</span></span>                                           |

| <span data-ttu-id="b50a3-2167">Attributo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b50a3-2167">Attribute</span></span>                                                                                    | <span data-ttu-id="b50a3-2168">Obbligatorio</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b50a3-2168">Mandatory</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="b50a3-2169">Derivato da</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b50a3-2169">Derived from</span></span>                                           |
